 duusare prastaav ke tahat mulaayam singh yadav ko sapa kaa sarvocch sangrakshak banaaya gaya, jabaki tisare prastaav ke tahat shivpal singh yadav ko sapa ke pradesh adhyaksh pad se tatkaal hataaya gaya or party mahasachiv amar singh ko sapa se tatkaal nishkasit kar diya gaya
 However, shortly before the commencement of the session, Mulayam issued a letter warning him of action against the leaders and activists who attended it, terming it as 'unconstitutional'
 mulaayam singh ne aanan-fanan main sapa ke sansadeey board kii baithak bulaai, jisamen adhiveshan ke tamaam faislon ko avaidh qaraar diya gaya
 He also expelled party vice-president Kiranmay Nanda and general secretary Naresh Aggarwal, along with Ram Gopal Yadav, the party's leader
 ramgopal ko shanivaar ko hi party main dobaaraa waapas liya gaya tha

 shivpal yadav dwaara 'twit' kiye gaye bina letters head vaale ek patr ke anusaar, sansadeey board kii baithak main sapa pramukh dwaara gat 28 disambar ko jari pratyaashiyon kii suchi ko anumodith karte hue bachi hui siton par ummidavaaron ke chayan ke liye mulaayam ko adhikrut kiya gaya
 According to the letter, the Parliamentary Board has also decided to convene the party's contingent national session on January 5 to remove the "confusion" that has spread after Sunday's session
 baharhaal, aaj ke adhiveshan ke baad akhilesh samarthak jabaran sapa karyaalay main ghus gaye or pradesh adhyaksh ke kaksh ke baahar lagi shivpal yadav kii nem plate ukhadkar phenk di
 Naresh Uttam Patel, the newly appointed state president, also took over his assignment immediately
 rashtriya adhyaksh banaae jane ke baad akhilesh yadav ne kaha ki vah hameshaa mulaayam singh kaa sammaan karte the or ab pehle se zyada sammaan karte hai

 If i have to make any sacrifice for the party, i will '

 a crisis arose again in the party
 unhone kaha ki party main tikaton kaa bantwaaraa manamaane dhang se hone laga tha

 tab yah nirnay liya gaya ki party kaa vishesh apatkaaleen adhiveshan bulaayaa jaae

 a post shared by Abhishek Bachchan (@bachchan) on Jun 10, 2017 at 11:02pm PDT # throwbackthursday taken in the mid 80's ( 1985 if memory serves)
 i call it Big b and the Bachchan bunch
 Dad was hospitalised with Mysthenia Gravis and my sister, cousins and i had gone to visit him
 Being too young to understand what all was going on our parents always made it out to be like an outing so that we would not be disturbed by the hospital and its workings
 When i used to visit my father after his accident on the sets of "coolie" in 1982, seeing him connected to many drips and machines, he used to tell me they were kites that he had got for me
 i was 6 yrs old
 My father was fighting for his life and all i thought about was
 
 
 why is he allowing me to play with these kites ??? The innocence of childhood i guess

 yah rishwat moin kuraishi cese main jaanch kar rahe adhikari vasuuli kaa racket chalaa rahe the, usee ke silsile main paisa diya gaya he
 We quickly tell you about the Moin Qureshi case
 maance vyapaaree hai moin akhtar kuraishi
 Their case has been going on for 7 years, three directors came during this but the matter did not reach the end
 2011 main upie kii sarkaar main jaanch shuru hui thi, chali gai, modi sarkaar aa gai or maamla vahiin kaa vahiin he balki is maamle ko lekar unke hi rajya mantri zad main aa gaye hai
 During this time, three directors of CBI came and went but the case of Moin Akhtar Qureshi did not reach the end
 raahat fateh ali khan moin kuraishi kii beti kii shaadi main aae the, lautate vakt airport par 56 lakh cash ke saath pakade gaye
 In the Lok Sabha elections, Prime Minister Modi also accused the Congress of this matter
 unki sarkaar aane ke teen saal baad sibiai ne cese darj kiya
 But its investigation overturned the CBI from within
 sibiai ke do-do nideshkon ke naam jaanch ke dauraan aa gaye
 And now Alok Verma and Rakesh Asthana face to face in this case
 nideshak e pi singh sibiai se ritair hokar upiessi ke member ban gaye the jahaan se inhen hataanaa padaa tha
 Satish Sana Moin was a friend of Qureshi and is also an accused in the Qureshi case
 sanaa asthana ko rishwat dene ke maamle main aaropee he
 Sana had alleged that he had given 2 crore to CBI Director Alok Verma through TDP MP CM Ramesh
 rakesh asthana sanaa ko hiraasat main lekar poochtacha karnaa chaahate the jisaki anumati alok verma ne nahin di, yah aarope he
 But when Sana recorded his statement, he said that he had given 3 crore to Rakesh Asthana in December 2017
 dubai ke vyapaaree manoj prasad or uske bhai somesh prasad ke zarie
 Based on this statement, an FIR was lodged against Asthana
 manoj prasad ko dilli main giraftaar kar liya gaya
 IPS officer Manish Kumar Sinha has accused Prime Minister Modi's minister of several crore bribes in connection with this case
 yah saamaanya nahin he ki sibiai ke diaiji ne na sirf koyala va khanan rajya mantri shri haribhaai parthi bhai choudhary par rishwat lene ke aarope lagaae balki isi maamle main pradhanmantri karyaalay or rashtriya suraksha salaahkaar ajit dobhaal par bhi baqayda likhit rup main apni yachika main aarope lagaae hai
 To interfere and influence in this case
 manish sinha ne kaha he ki jis asthana cese ko wo dekh rahe the, usase hataakar unka tabadalaa nagpur isliye kiya gaya kyonki piemo ke ishaare par shaktishaalee logon ko bachaaya ja rahaa tha
 Evidence was possible
 manish sinha neerav modi or mehul chaukasee kaa bhi cese dekh rahe the
 Has National Security Advisor Ajit Doval interfered in Asthana's investigation, preventing Asthana from raiding and confiscating his phone to save him? Manish Kumar Sinha has written in his petition that the National Security Advisor at several levels created a deadlock in the investigation against Asthana
 is cese main shaamil do midileman ajit dobhaal ke kareebi the
 It was through Dubai middle man Manoj that he was accused of giving money to Asthana, after his arrest Manoj wondered how the CBI could hold him while he was close to Ajit Doval
 uske bhai somesh or ro ke adhikari samant goyal ne ek personal cese main ajit dobhaal kii madad kii thi
 From the investigation against Asthana to the FIR level, Ajit Doval was interested
 yachika main likhaa he ki 5 aktubar ko asthana ke khilaaf exiaar hui thi jisaki soochna alok verma ne ajit dobhaal ko 17 aktubar ko di
 The question is why Alok Verma was telling Ajit Doval that an FIR has been lodged against Asthana and why Ajit Doval was telling Asthana that an FIR has been lodged against you
 kya asthana ne ajit dobhaal se guzarish kii thi ki unki giraftaar nahin honi chahie or ajit dobhaal ne asthana ko giraftaar hone se bachaa liya, yah sab yachika main likhaa gaya he, khandan se to baat nahin banegi, yah maamla ab jaanch se bhi aage kaa ho gaya he
 It has been written in the petition that under the pressure of Ajit Doval, permission was not given to search Asthana's house and his mobile phone was not confiscated
 jaanch adhikari e ke bassi ne aarope lagaae hai, em ke sinha ne apni yachika main yah sab likhaa he ki alok verma ne poochne par kaha ki rashtriya suraksha salaahkaar ne cell phone zabt karne kii anumati nahin di
 a formal request was made to Alok Verma on 22 October but permission was not granted again
